# ::id dip_test_0001.1
# ::snt ITALY message AUSTRIA that Hey Austria! I know AT is one of the least successful alliances in the game, so I'm super down to work together here, especially if we can get Russia and Turkey fighting.
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Italy"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Austria"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c2
                        :op2 c)
                  :ARG3 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Italy")))
            :ARG2 c2)
      :ARG3 c3)

# ::id dip_test_0001.2
# ::snt FRANCE message GERMANY that Hey Germany! Just reaching out to say I think our two nations tend to benefit a ton from working together, and I'm very down to work together if you'd be interested!
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany"))))
            :ARG2 c2)
      :ARG3 c2)

# ::id dip_test_0001.3
# ::snt FRANCE message ITALY that Hey Italy! I think our two nations tend to do best when we can leave each other alone, so I'd love it if we could agree to not harass one another?
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (a / attack-01
                  :polarity -
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Italy")))
            :ARG2 c3)
      :ARG3 c2)

# ::id dip_test_0001.4
# ::snt GERMANY message FRANCE that Hey France, absolutely! Are you up for a DMZ in Burgundy?
(t / tell-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Germany"))
      :ARG1 (a / and
            :op1 (p / propose-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "France"))
                  :ARG1 (d / demilitarize-01
                        :ARG1 a
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG2 (s / sea
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "English"
                              :op2 "Channel")))
            :ARG3 c)
      :op2 (t2 / threaten-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (c3 / country
                  :name (n4 / name
                        :op1 "France"))
            :ARG2 c3))

# ::id dip_test_0001.5
# ::snt TURKEY message RUSSIA that Hey Russia, just wanna say good luck and hopefully we can be friends!
(t / tell-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country

                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c

                                    :op1 "Russia"))))
            :ARG3 c)
      :ARG2 c3)

# ::id dip_test_0001.6
# ::snt AUSTRIA message ITALY that I'm also down! Have you heard from either of them yet?
(t / tell-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG1 (s / support-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (m / move-01
                  :ARG1 (u / unit
                        :mod (c2 / country
                              :name (n2 / name
                                    :op1 "Italy")))
                  :ARG2 (p / province
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Tunisia"))))
      :ARG2 (c3 / country
            :name (n4 / name
                  :op1 "Germany")))

# ::id dip_test_0001.7
# ::snt ENGLAND message FRANCE that Hey France! I think we both have bigger concerns than each other so I'd like to propose an alliance between us. Would you be willing to agree to a DMZ in the Channel?

      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "England"))
      :ARG1 (p2 / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Germany"))
            :ARG1 (a / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c2
                        :op2 c))
            :ARG3 (c3 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "France")))
      :ARG3 c2)

      :ARG3 c2)

# ::id dip_test_0001.12
# ::snt FRANCE message ENGLAND that Hey England! I'm more than happy to agree to that, I think our nations tend to do best when we don't harass one another. Would you like to focus together on attacking Germany, or would you rather move in separate directions?
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "France"))
            :ARG1 (a2 / agree-01
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (a3 / attack-01
                        :ARG0 (a4 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "England")))
                        :ARG1 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany")))
                  :ARG2 c2)
            :ARG2 c3)
      :op2 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 c3
            :ARG1 (a5 / attack-01
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 (c4 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Germany")))
            :ARG3 c)
      :ARG3 c4)

# ::id dip_test_0001.19
# ::snt ENGLAND message RUSSIA that Hey Russia! I'd like to take Norway this year, but I'm not planning on sending any further units your way. If there's anything I can do to help you, feel free to ask!
(a / and
      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (t / tell-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Russia"))
                  :ARG1 (h / have-03
                        :ARG0 c
                        :ARG1 (p2 / province
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Norway"))
                        :time (d / date-entity
                              :year 1902))
                  :ARG2 (c3 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Russia")))
            :ARG3 c2)
      :op2 (p3 / propose-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (t2 / tell-01
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 h
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 p2
                  :time d
                  :year 1902)
            :ARG2 c3)
      :ARG3 c3)

                  :op1 (d / demilitarize-01

                              :name (n6 / name
                                    :op1 "Piedmont"))

# ::id dip_test_0001.31
# ::snt ENGLAND message RUSSIA that I don't think I can do that; it would leave me completely open to France. However, I am planning on taking it with a fleet.

      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))

                  :polarity -
                  :ARG1 (h / have-03
                        :ARG0 c
                        :ARG1 (p2 / province
                              :name (n2 / name
                                    :op1 "Marseille"))))
            :ARG2 (c2 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Russia")))
      :op2 t
      :ARG0 c
      :ARG1 (p3 / possible-01
            :ARG1 (h2 / have-03
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (p4 / province
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Burgundy"))))
      :ARG2 c2
      :op3 (e / expect-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (h3 / have-03
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 p4)))

# ::id dip_test_0001.32
# ::snt RUSSIA message AUSTRIA that Hey Austria, sounds good to me! Bounce Galicia and work together sounds good to me, I think the R/A is one of the more powerful alliances on the board.

      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Russia"))
            :ARG1 (p / propose-01
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (b / bounce-03
                        :ARG1 (u / unit
                              :mod c)
                        :ARG2 (u2 / unit
                              :mod (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "Austria")))
                        :ARG3 (p2 / province
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Galicia")))
                  :ARG3 c2)
            :ARG2 c2)
      :op2 (a2 / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a3 / and
                  :op1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Italy"))
                  :op2 c)))

(t / tell-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG1 (b / build-01
            :polarity -
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (u / unit)
            :location (p / province
                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Ankara")))
      :ARG2 (c2 / country
            :name (n3 / name
                  :op1 "Italy")))

                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Russia")))
      :op2 (t2 / tell-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 h
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 s)
      :ARG2 c2)

                              :op1 c
                              :op2 c2))
                  :ARG2 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Austria")))
            :ARG2 c3)
      :ARG3 c2)
